 Mi Air Purifier 3 launched in India
 haal hi main launch kiya gaya tha bajet air purifire
 Chinese tech company Xiaomi has launched a new air purifier in India
 ye Air Purifier 3 he or isaki keemat xxrep 4 9 rupee he
 Recently the company has launched Mi Air Purifier 2C in India
 company ne kaha he ki nae air purifire main kai impruvement kiye gaye hai or kuch nae fitures bhi shaamil kiye gaye hai
 You can buy Mi Air Purifier 3 from Amazon India and Flipkart
 bikri 7 november yani kal se shuru hogi
 Apart from this, the company will also continue to sell the Mi Purifier 2C and its other air purifiers
 company ne kaha he ki isamen HEPA Class 13 filter diya gaya he
 Talking about the features of MI Air Purifier 3, the company has said that it has a triple layer filtration system
 inamen se ek HEPA Class 13 filter he, ek activited carbon filter he
 It has a touch screen OLED display where the necessary information is visible
 company kaa daawa he ki yah air purifire 380 cubic meter prati ghante kaa CADR deliver karata he
 CADR ie Clean Air Delivery Rate
 Mi Air Purifier 3 ko google assistant or Amazon Alexa ke saath bhi conect kar sakate hai
 In the design, it is not much difference from the previous Xiaomi air purifiers
 company ne ye bhi daawa kiya he ye isamen diya gaya HEPA filter hawa ke chote polyants ko khatm karata he or ise 99
 Reduces up to 9%
 shaomi ke mutabik isamen 360 degree selindrical filter dizin diya gaya he jo chaaron taraf se hawa ko abjorv karke ise filter karata he
 It has an activated carbon filter that eliminates toxic toxic substances and odor of air
